<p><strong>Features</strong></p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Focus is managed and can be customized</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Supports modal and non-modal modes</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Ensures correct DOM order after tabbing out of the popover, whether it&#x27;s
portalled or not</li>
</ul>

<h2 id="anatomy" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Anatomy<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#anatomy"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Check the popover anatomy and part names.</p>

<h2 id="usage" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Usage<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#usage"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Import the popover package:</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword module">import</span> <span class="token imports"><span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token keyword module">as</span> popover</span> <span class="token keyword module">from</span> <span class="token string">&quot;@zag-js/popover&quot;</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>The popover package exports two key functions:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">machine</code> - State machine logic.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">connect</code> - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.</li>
</ul>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p>Pass a unique <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">id</code> to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">useMachine</code> so generated element ids stay predictable.</p>
</blockquote>
<p>Then use the framework integration helpers:</p>
<div data-scope="tabs" data-part="root" id="tabs:popover/usage.mdx" data-orientation="horizontal" dir="ltr" class="w_full max-w_768px bd-w_1px my_8 bg_bg.code.block bdr_6px"><div data-scope="tabs" <h3 id="rendering-the-popover-in-a-portal" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Rendering the popover in a portal<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#rendering-the-popover-in-a-portal"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>By default, the popover is rendered in the same DOM hierarchy as the trigger. To
render the popover within a portal, pass <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">portalled: true</code> property to the
machine&#x27;s context.</p>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p>Note: This requires that you render the component within a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">Portal</code> based on
the framework you use.</p>
</blockquote>

</span></div></pre><button type="button" class="px_2 py_1 gap_1 bd-w_1px pos_absolute right_5 top_3 d_flex ai_center fs_xs bg_bg.subtle bd-c_border.subtle cursor_pointer hover:bg_bg.muted"><svg stroke="currentColor" fill="none" stroke-width="2" viewBox="0 0 24 24" aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="w_1em h_1em va_middle" height="1em" width="1em" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="M8 5H6a2 2 0 00-2 2v12a2 2 0 002 2h10a2 2 0 002-2v-1M8 5a2 2 0 002 2h2a2 2 0 002-2M8 5a2 2 0 012-2h2a2 2 0 012 2m0 0h2a2 2 0 012 2v3m2 4H10m0 0l3-3m-3 3l3 3"></path></svg><span>Copy</span></button></div></div></div>
<h3 id="managing-focus-within-popover" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Managing focus within popover<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#managing-focus-within-popover"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the popover opens, focus moves to the first focusable element. To customize
this, set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">initialFocusEl</code>.</p>

<p>To disable automatic focus on open, set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">autoFocus</code> to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">false</code>.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>popover<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">autoFocus</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">false</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="changing-the-modality" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Changing the modality<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#changing-the-modality"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>In some cases, you might want the popover to be <strong>modal</strong>. This means that
it&#x27;ll:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">trap focus within its content</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">block scrolling on the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">body</code></li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">disable pointer interactions outside the popover</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">hide content behind the popover from screen readers</li>
</ul>
<p>To make the popover modal, set the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">modal: true</code> property in the machine&#x27;s
context. When <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">modal: true</code>, we set the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">portalled</code> attribute to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">true</code> as well.</p>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p><strong>Note</strong>: This requires that you render the component within a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">Portal</code>.</p>
</blockquote>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>popover<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">modal</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="close-behavior" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Close behavior<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#close-behavior"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The popover is designed to close on blur and when the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">esc</code> key is pressed.</p>
<p>To prevent it from closing on blur (clicking or focusing outside), pass the
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">closeOnInteractOutside</code> property and set it to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">false</code>.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>popover<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">closeOnInteractOutside</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">false</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>To prevent it from closing when the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">esc</code> key is pressed, pass the
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">closeOnEscape</code> property and set it to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">false</code>.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>popover<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">closeOnEscape</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">false</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="controlled-open-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Controlled open state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#controlled-open-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">open</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onOpenChange</code> to control visibility externally.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>popover<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  open<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">onOpenChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token function">setOpen</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">open</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="adding-an-arrow" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Adding an arrow<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#adding-an-arrow"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>To render an arrow within the popover, use the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api.getArrowProps()</code> and
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api.getArrowTipProps()</code>.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">//...</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> api <span class="token operator">=</span> popover<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">connect</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>service<span class="token punctuation">,</span> normalizeProps<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword control-flow">return</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>

</span></span><span class="code-line highlight-line"><span class="token plain-text">    </span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>div</span> <span class="token spread"><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token spread operator">...</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getContentProps</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token plain-text">
</span></span><span class="code-line highlight-line"><span class="token plain-text">      </span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>div</span> <span class="token spread"><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token spread operator">...</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getArrowProps</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token plain-text">
</span></span><span class="code-line highlight-line"><span class="token plain-text">        </span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>div</span> <span class="token spread"><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token spread operator">...</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getArrowTipProps</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span> <span class="token punctuation">/&gt;</span></span><span class="token plain-text">
</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token plain-text">      </span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>div</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token plain-text">

</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token plain-text">  </span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>div</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">//...</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="changing-the-placement" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Changing the placement<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#changing-the-placement"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>To change the placement of the popover, set the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">positioning.placement</code> property
in the machine&#x27;s context.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>popover<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">positioning</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token literal-property property">placement</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;top-start&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="listening-for-open-state-changes" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Listening for open state changes<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#listening-for-open-state-changes"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the popover is opened or closed, the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onOpenChange</code> callback is invoked.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>popover<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token function">onOpenChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token comment">// details =&gt; { open: boolean }</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;Popover&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">open</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="usage-within-dialog" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Usage within dialog<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#usage-within-dialog"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When using the popover within a dialog, avoid rendering the popover in a
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">Portal</code> or <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">Teleport</code>. This is because the dialog will trap focus within it,
and the popover will be rendered outside the dialog.</p>
<h2 id="styling-guide" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Styling guide<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#styling-guide"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Each part includes a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-part</code> attribute you can target in CSS.</p>
<h3 id="open-and-closed-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Open and closed state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#open-and-closed-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the popover is expanded, we add a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-state</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-placement</code>
attribute to the trigger.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;trigger&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-state</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;open|closed&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for the expanded state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;content&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-state</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;open|closed&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for the expanded state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;trigger&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-placement</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;(top|bottom)-(start|end)&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for computed placement */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="position-aware" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Position aware<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#position-aware"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the popover is expanded, <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-placement</code> is added to trigger and content.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;trigger&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-placement</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;(top|bottom)-(start|end)&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for computed placement */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;content&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-placement</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;(top|bottom)-(start|end)&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for computed placement */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="arrow" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Arrow<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#arrow"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The arrow element requires specific css variables to be set for it to show
correctly.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;arrow&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token variable">--arrow-background</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> <span class="token color">white</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token variable">--arrow-size</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> <span class="token number">16</span><span class="token unit">px</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>A common technique for adding a shadow to the arrow is to use
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">filter: drop-shadow(...)</code> on the content element. Alternatively, you can use
the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">--arrow-shadow-color</code> variable.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;arrow&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token variable">--arrow-shadow-color</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> <span class="token color">gray</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="methods-and-properties" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Methods and Properties<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#methods-and-properties"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<h3 id="machine-context" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine Context<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-context"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The popover machine exposes the following context properties:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">ids</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">Partial&lt;{ anchor: string; trigger: string; content: string; title: string; description: string; closeTrigger: string; positioner: string; arrow: string; }&gt;</code><span class="d_block">The ids of the elements in the popover. Useful for composition.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">modal</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the popover should be modal. When set to `true`:
- interaction with outside elements will be disabled
- only popover content will be visible to screen readers
- scrolling is blocked
- focus is trapped within the popover</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">portalled</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the popover is portalled. This will proxy the tabbing behavior regardless of the DOM position
of the popover content.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">autoFocus</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether to automatically set focus on the first focusable
content within the popover when opened.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">initialFocusEl</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">() =&gt; HTMLElement</code><span class="d_block">The element to focus on when the popover is opened.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">closeOnInteractOutside</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether to close the popover when the user clicks outside of the popover.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">closeOnEscape</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether to close the popover when the escape key is pressed.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onOpenChange</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: OpenChangeDetails) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function invoked when the popover opens or closes</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">positioning</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">PositioningOptions</code><span class="d_block">The user provided options used to position the popover content</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">open</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">The controlled open state of the popover</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultOpen</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">The initial open state of the popover when rendered.
Use when you don&#x27;t need to control the open state of the popover.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">id</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The unique identifier of the machine.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getRootNode</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">() =&gt; Node | ShadowRoot | Document</code><span class="d_block">A root node to correctly resolve document in custom environments. E.x.: Iframes, Electron.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">dir</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">&quot;ltr&quot; | &quot;rtl&quot;</code><span class="d_block">The document&#x27;s text/writing direction.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onEscapeKeyDown</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(event: KeyboardEvent) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function called when the escape key is pressed</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onRequestDismiss</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(event: LayerDismissEvent) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function called when this layer is closed due to a parent layer being closed</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onPointerDownOutside</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(event: PointerDownOutsideEvent) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function called when the pointer is pressed down outside the component</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onFocusOutside</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(event: FocusOutsideEvent) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function called when the focus is moved outside the component</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onInteractOutside</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(event: InteractOutsideEvent) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function called when an interaction happens outside the component</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">persistentElements</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(() =&gt; Element)[]</code><span class="d_block">Returns the persistent elements that:
- should not have pointer-events disabled
- should not trigger the dismiss event</span></li></ul>
<h3 id="machine-api" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine API<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-api"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The popover <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api</code> exposes the following methods:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">portalled</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the popover is portalled.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">open</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the popover is open</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">setOpen</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(open: boolean) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function to open or close the popover</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">reposition</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(options?: Partial&lt;PositioningOptions&gt;) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function to reposition the popover</span></li></ul>
<h3 id="data-attributes" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Data Attributes<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#data-attributes"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>

<h2 id="accessibility" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Accessibility<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#accessibility"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Adheres to the
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener" href="https://www.w3.org/WAI/ARIA/apg/patterns/dialogmodal" class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px">Dialog WAI-ARIA design pattern</a>.</p>
<h3 id="keyboard-interactions" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Keyboard Interactions<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#keyboard-interactions"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>

bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">Tab</kbd></div><div><span>Moves focus to the next focusable element within the content.<br /><strong>Note:</strong> If there are no focusable elements, focus is moved to the next focusable element after the trigger.</span></div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block element within the content<br /><strong>Note:</strong> If there are no focusable elements, focus is moved to the trigger.</span></div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 It is used to\ndisplay contextual information to the user, and should be paired with a\nclickable trigger element.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cresources pkg=\"@zag-js/popover\"\u003e\n\u003cshowcase id=\"Popover\"\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eFeatures\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eFocus is managed and can be customized\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSupports modal and non-modal modes\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eEnsures correct DOM order after tabbing out of the popover, whether it's\nportalled or not\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eInstallation\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eInstall the popover package:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ccodesnippet id=\"popover/installation.mdx\"\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eAnatomy\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eCheck the popover anatomy and part names.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cblockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eEach part includes a \u003ccode\u003edata-part\u003c/code\u003e attribute to help identify them in the DOM.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/blockquote\u003e\n\u003canatomy id=\"popover\"\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eUsage\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eImport the popover package:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003eimport * as popover from \"@zag-js/popover\"\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe popover package exports two key functions:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003emachine\u003c/code\u003e - State machine logic.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003econnect\u003c/code\u003e - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cblockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003ePass a unique \u003ccode\u003eid\u003c/code\u003e to \u003ccode\u003euseMachine\u003c/code\u003e so generated element ids stay predictable.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/blockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThen use the framework integration helpers:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ccodesnippet id=\"popover/usage.mdx\"\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eRendering the popover in a portal\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eBy default, the popover is rendered in the same DOM hierarchy as the trigger. To\nrender the popover within a portal, pass \u003ccode\u003eportalled: true\u003c/code\u003e property to the\nmachine's context.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cblockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eNote: This requires that you render the component within a \u003ccode\u003ePortal\u003c/code\u003e based on\nthe framework you use.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/blockquote\u003e\n\u003ccodesnippet id=\"popover/render-in-portal.mdx\"\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eManaging focus within popover\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWhen the popover opens, focus moves to the first focusable element. To customize\nthis, set \u003ccode\u003einitialFocusEl\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ccodesnippet id=\"popover/initial-focus.mdx\"\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo disable automatic focus on open, set \u003ccode\u003eautoFocus\u003c/code\u003e to \u003ccode\u003efalse\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(popover.machine, {\n  autoFocus: false,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eChanging the modality\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eIn some cases, you might want the popover to be \u003cstrong\u003emodal\u003c/strong\u003e. This means that\nit'll:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003etrap focus within its content\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eblock scrolling on the \u003ccode\u003ebody\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003edisable pointer interactions outside the popover\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003ehide content behind the popover from screen readers\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo make the popover modal, set the \u003ccode\u003emodal: true\u003c/code\u003e property in the machine's\ncontext. When \u003ccode\u003emodal: true\u003c/code\u003e, we set the \u003ccode\u003eportalled\u003c/code\u003e attribute to \u003ccode\u003etrue\u003c/code\u003e as \u003ccode\u003ePortal\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/blockquote\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(popover.machine, {\n  modal: true,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eClose behavior\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe popover is designed to close on blur and when the \u003ccode\u003eesc\u003c/code\u003e key is pressed.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo prevent it from closing on blur (clicking or focusing outside), pass metastring=\"{6-8}\"\u003e//...\nconst api = popover.connect(service, normalizeProps)\n//...\nreturn (\n  \u0026#x3C;div {...api.getPositionerProps()}\u003e\n    \u0026#x3C;div {...api.getContentProps()}\u003e\n      \u0026#x3C;div {...api.getArrowProps()}\u003e\n        \u0026#x3C;div {...api.getArrowTipProps()} /\u003e\n      \u0026#x3C;/div\u003e\n      //...\n likely forgot to import, pass, or provide it.\")}"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"12:T17fd,"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"A popover is a non-modal dialog that floats around a trigger. It is used to\ndisplay contextual information to the user, and should be paired with a\nclickable trigger element.\n\n\u003cResources pkg=\"@zag-js/popover\" /\u003e\n\n\u003cShowcase id=\"Popover\" /\u003e\n\n**Features**\n\n- Focus is managed and can be customized\n- Supports modal and non-modal modes\n- Ensures correct DOM order after tabbing out of the popover, whether it's\n  portalled or not\n\n## Installation\n\nInstall the popover package:\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"popover/installation.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n## Anatomy\n\nCheck the popover anatomy and part names.\n\n\u003e Each part includes a `data-part` attribute to help identify them in the DOM.\n\n\u003cAnatomy id=\"popover\" /\u003e\n\n## Usage\n\nImport the popover package:\n\n```jsx\nimport * as popover from \"@zag-js/popover\"\n```\n\nThe popover package exports two key functions:\n\n- `machine` - State machine logic.\n- `connect` - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.\n\n\u003e Pass a unique `id` to `useMachine` so generated element ids stay predictable.\n\nThen use the framework integration helpers:\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"popover/usage.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n### Rendering the popover in a portal\n\nBy default, the popover is rendered in the same DOM hierarchy as the trigger. To\nrender the popover within a portal, pass `portalled: true` property to the\nmachine's context.\n\n\u003e Note: This requires that you render the component within a `Portal` based on\n\u003e the framework you use.\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"popover/render-in-portal.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n### Managing focus within popover\n\nWhen the popover opens, focus moves to the first focusable element. To customize\nthis, set `initialFocusEl`.\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"popover/initial-focus.mdx\" /\u003e\n\nTo disable automatic focus on open, set `autoFocus` to `false`.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(popover.machine, {\n  autoFocus: false,\n})\n```\n\n### Changing the modality\n\nIn some cases, you might want the popover to be **modal**. This means that\nit'll:\n\n- trap focus within its content\n- block scrolling on the `body`\n- disable pointer interactions outside the popover\n- hide content behind the popover from screen readers\n\nTo make the popover modal, set the `modal: true` property in the machine's\ncontext. When `modal: true`, we set the `portalled` attribute to `true` as well.\n\n\u003e **Note**: This requires that you render the component within a `Portal`.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(popover.machine, {\n  modal: true,\n})\n```\n\n### Close behavior\n\nThe popover is designed to close on blur and when the `esc` key is pressed.\n\nTo prevent it from closing on blur (clicking or focusing outside), pass the\n`closeOnInteractOutside` property and set it to `false`.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(popover.machine, {\n  closeOnInteractOutside: false,\n})\n```\n\nTo prevent it from closing when the `esc` key is pressed, pass the\n`closeOnEscape` property and set it to `false`.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(popover.machine, {\n  closeOnEscape: false,\n})\n```\n\n### Controlled open state\n\nUse `open` and `onOpenChange` to control visibility externally.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(popover.machine, {\n  open,\n  onOpenChange(details) {\n    setOpen(details.open)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Adding an arrow\n\nTo render an arrow within the popover, use the `api.getArrowProps()` and\n`api.getArrowTipProps()`.\n\n```jsx {6-8}\n//...\nconst api = popover.connect(service, normalizeProps)\n//...\nreturn (\n  \u003cdiv {...api.getPositionerProps()}\u003e\n    \u003cdiv {...api.getContentProps()}\u003e\n      \u003cdiv {...api.getArrowProps()}\u003e\n        \u003cdiv {...api.getArrowTipProps()} /\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n      //...\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n)\n//...\n```\n\n### Changing the placement\n\nTo change the placement of the popover, set the `positioning.placement` property\nin the machine's context.\n\n```jsx {2-4}\nconst service = useMachine(popover.machine, {\n  positioning: {\n    placement: \"top-start\",\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Listening for open state changes\n\nWhen the popover is opened or closed, the `onOpenChange` callback is invoked.\n\n```jsx {2-7}\nconst service = useMachine(popover.machine, {\n  onOpenChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { open: boolean }\n    console.log(\"Popover\", details.open)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Usage within dialog\n\nWhen using the popover within a dialog, avoid rendering the popover in a\n`Portal` or `Teleport`. This is because the dialog will trap focus within it,\nand the popover will be rendered outside the dialog.\n\n## Styling guide\n\nEach part includes a `data-part` attribute you can target in CSS.\n\n### Open and closed state\n\nWhen the popover is expanded, we add a `data-state` and `data-placement`\nattribute to the trigger.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"trigger\"][data-state=\"open|closed\"] {\n  /* styles for the expanded state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"content\"][data-state=\"open|closed\"] {\n  /* styles for the expanded state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"trigger\"][data-placement=\"(top|bottom)-(start|end)\"] {\n  /* styles for computed placement */\n}\n```\n\n### Position aware\n\nWhen the popover is expanded, `data-placement` is added to trigger and content.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"trigger\"][data-placement=\"(top|bottom)-(start|end)\"] {\n  /* styles for computed placement */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"content\"][data-placement=\"(top|bottom)-(start|end)\"] {\n  /* styles for computed placement */\n}\n```\n\n### Arrow\n\nThe arrow element requires specific css variables to be set for it to show\ncorrectly.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"arrow\"] {\n  --arrow-background: white;\n  --arrow-size: 16px;\n}\n```\n\nA common technique for adding a shadow to the arrow is to use\n`filter: drop-shadow(...)` on the content element. Alternatively, you can use\nthe `--arrow-shadow-color` variable.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"arrow\"] {\n  --arrow-shadow-color: gray;\n}\n```\n\n## Methods and Properties\n\n### Machine Context\n\nThe popover machine exposes the following context properties:\n\n\u003cContextTable name=\"popover\" /\u003e\n\n### Machine API\n\nThe popover `api` exposes the following methods:\n\n\u003cApiTable name=\"popover\" /\u003e\n\n### Data Attributes\n\n\u003cDataAttrTable name=\"popover\" /\u003e\n\n### CSS Variables\n\n\u003cCssVarTable name=\"popover\" /\u003e\n\n## Accessibility\n\nAdheres to the\n[Dialog WAI-ARIA design pattern](https://www.w3.org/WAI/ARIA/apg/patterns/dialogmodal).\n\n### Keyboard Interactions\n\n\u003cKeyboardTable name=\"popover\" /\u003e"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"5:[\"$\",\"$Le\",null,{\"doc\":{\"title\":\"Popover\",\"description\":\"Using the popover machine in your
